में लॉगिन करें और 'सिंक' और 'बैकअप' के तहत स्थित बैकअप को हटा दें","تسجيل الدخول إلى حساب Google الخاص بك وحذف النسخ الاحتياطية الموجودة تحت ""Sync"" و ""النسخ الاحتياطية""","Faça login na sua conta do Google e exclua backups localizados em 'Sync' e 'Backups'","Войдите в свою учетную запись Google и удалите резервные копии, расположенные под «синхронизацией» и «резервными копиями»","Googleアカウントにログインし、「同期」と「バックアップ」の下にあるバックアップを削除します","Melden Sie sich in Ihrem Google -Konto an und löschen","Google 계정에 로그인하고 'Sync'및 'Backups'에있는 백업을 삭제합니다.","Google hesabınıza giriş yapın ve 'senkronizasyon' ve 'yedeklemeler' altında bulunan yedeklemeleri silin","Accedi al tuo account Google ed elimina i backup situati in ""Sync"" e ""Backups""","Đăng nhập vào tài khoản Google của bạn và xóa các bản sao lưu nằm trong 'Sync' và 'Sao lưu'","Zaloguj się na swoje konto Google i usuń kopie zapasowe znajdujące się pod „Sync” i „Backups”","Log in op uw Google -account en verwijder back -ups onder 'Sync' en 'back -ups'","เข้าสู่ระบบบัญชี Google ของคุณและลบการสำรองข้อมูลที่อยู่ภายใต้ 'ซิงค์' และ 'การสำรองข้อมูล'","Přihlaste se k vašemu účtu Google a smažte zálohy umístěné pod „synchronizací“ a „zálohy“","আপনার গুগল অ্যাকাউন্টে লগইন করুন এবং 'সিঙ্ক' এবং 'ব্যাকআপস' এর অধীনে অবস্থিত ব্যাকআপগুলি মুছুন","Masuk ke akun Google Anda dan hapus cadangan yang terletak di bawah 'Sync' dan 'Backups'","اپنے گوگل اکاؤنٹ میں لاگ ان کریں اور 'مطابقت پذیری' اور 'بیک اپ' کے تحت واقع بیک اپ کو حذف کریں","మీ Google ఖాతాకు లాగిన్ అవ్వండి మరియు 'సమకాలీకరణ' మరియు 'బ్యాకప్‌లు' కింద ఉన్న బ్యాకప్‌లను తొలగించండి","आपल्या Google खात्यावर लॉग इन करा आणि 'समक्रमण' आणि 'बॅकअप' अंतर्गत स्थित बॅकअप हटवा","உங்கள் Google கணக்கில் உள்நுழைந்து 'ஒத்திசைவு' மற்றும் 'காப்புப்பிரதிகள்' ஆகியவற்றின் கீழ் அமைந்துள்ள காப்புப்பிரதிகளை நீக்கவும்","તમારા Google એકાઉન્ટ પર લ Login ગિન કરો અને 'સિંક' અને 'બેકઅપ્સ' હેઠળ સ્થિત બેકઅપ્સ કા delete ી નાખો","Увійдіть до свого облікового запису Google та видаліть резервні копії, розташовані під ""синхронізацією"" та ""резервні копії""","Mag -login sa iyong Google account at tanggalin ang mga backup na matatagpuan sa ilalim ng 'Sync' at 'Backups'","Log masuk ke akaun Google anda dan padamkan sandaran yang terletak di bawah 'Sync' dan 'Backups'","Conectați -vă la contul dvs. Google și ștergeți backup -urile situate în „Sync” și „Backup -uri”","Jelentkezzen be a Google -fiókjába, és törölje a „Sync” és a „Backups” alatt található biztonsági mentéseket","Συνδεθείτε στο λογαριασμό σας στο Google και διαγράψτε τα αντίγραφα ασφαλείας που βρίσκονται στο ""συγχρονισμό"" και ""Backups""","Logga in på ditt Google -konto och ta bort säkerhetskopior som finns under 'Sync' och 'Backups'","Log ind på din Google -konto og slet sikkerhedskopier placeret under 'Sync' og 'Backups'","Logg inn på Google -kontoen din og slett sikkerhetskopier som ligger under 'Sync' og 'Backups'","Kirjaudu Google -tiliisi ja poista varmuuskopiot, jotka sijaitsevat 'synkronoinnissa' ja 'varmuuskopiot'","התחבר לחשבון Google שלך ​​ומחק גיבויים הממוקמים תחת 'סנכרון' ו'גיבויים '","وارد حساب Google خود شوید و نسخه پشتیبان تهیه شده در زیر ""Sync"" و ""Backups"" را حذف کنید","നിങ്ങളുടെ Google അക്ക to ണ്ടിലേക്ക് പ്രവേശിച്ച് 'സമന്വയ', 'ബാക്കപ്പുകൾ' എന്നിവയിൽ സ്ഥിതിചെയ്യുന്ന ബാക്കപ്പുകൾ ഇല്ലാതാക്കുക","Пријавите се на свој Гоогле налог и избришите сигурносне копије које се налазе под 'Синц' и 'Резервне копије'","Ingia kwenye akaunti yako ya Google na futa backups ziko chini ya 'Usawazishaji' na 'Backups'"

கீழ் அமைந்துள்ள காப்புப்பிரதிகளை நீக்கவும்","તમારા Google એકાઉન્ટ પર લ Login ગિન કરો અને 'સિંક' અને 'બેકઅપ્સ' હેઠળ સ્થિત બેકઅપ્સ કા delete ી નાખો","Увійдіть до свого облікового запису Google та видаліть резервні копії, розташовані під ""синхронізацією"" та ""резервні копії""","Mag -login sa iyong Google account at tanggalin ang mga backup na matatagpuan sa ilalim ng 'Sync' at 'Backups'","Log masuk ke akaun Google anda dan padamkan sandaran yang terletak di bawah 'Sync' dan 'Backups'","Conectați -vă la contul dvs. Google și ștergeți backup -urile situate în „Sync” și „Backup ""Backups"" را حذف کنید","നിങ്ങളുടെ Google അക്ക to ണ്ടിലേക്ക് പ്രവേശിച്ച് 'സമന്വയ', 'ബാക്കപ്പുകൾ' എന്നിവയിൽ സ്ഥിതിചെയ്യുന്ന ബാക്കപ്പുകൾ ഇല്ലാതാക്കുക","Пријавите се на свој Гоогле налог и избришите +Future<bool> setHighRefreshRate() async {
+  try {
+    if (getPlatform() == PlatformOS.isAndroid)
+      await FlutterDisplayMode.setHighRefreshRate();
+    return true;
+  } catch (e) {
+    print("Error setting high refresh rate: " + e.toString());
+  }
+  return false;

+class LinkInNotes extends StatelessWidget {
+  const LinkInNotes({
+    required this.link,
+    required this.onTap,
+    this.onLongPress,
+    this.iconData,
+    this.iconDataAfter,
+    this.color,
+    super.key,
+  });
+  final String link;
+  final VoidCallback onTap;
+  final VoidCallback? onLongPress;
+  final IconData? iconData;
+  final IconData? iconDataAfter;
+  final Color? color;
+
+  @override
+  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
+    return Tappable(
+      onTap: onTap,
+      onLongPress: onLongPress,
+      color: color ??
+          darkenPastel(
+              (appStateSettings["materialYou"]
+                  ? Theme.of(context).colorScheme.secondaryContainer
+                  : getColor(context, "canvasContainer")),
+              amount: 0.2),
+      child: Padding(
+        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 15, vertical: 10),
+        child: Row(
+          children: [
+            Icon(
+              iconData ??
+                  (appStateSettings["outlinedIcons"]
+                      ? Icons.link_outlined
+                      : Icons.link_rounded),
+            ),
+            SizedBox(width: 10),
+            Expanded(
+              child: TextFont(
+                text: link
+                    .replaceFirst("www.", "")
+                    .replaceFirst("http://", "")
+                    .replaceFirst("https://", ""),
+                fontSize: 16,
+                maxLines: 1,
+              ),
+            ),
+            if (iconDataAfter != null) Icon(iconDataAfter),
+          ],
+        ),
+      ),
+    );
+  }

+Future<String?> getPhotoAndUpload({required ImageSource source}) async {
+  dynamic result = await openLoadingPopupTryCatch(() async {
+    final ImagePicker picker = ImagePicker();
+    final XFile? photo = await picker.pickImage(source: source);
+    if (photo == null)
+      throw (
+        source == ImageSource.camera
+            ? "no-photo-taken".tr()
+            : "no-file-selected".tr(),
+      );
+
+    var fileBytes;
+    late Stream<List<int>> mediaStream;
+    fileBytes = await photo.readAsBytes();
+    mediaStream = Stream.value(List<int>.from(fileBytes));
+
+    try {
+      return await uploadFileToDrive(
+          fileBytes: fileBytes, fileName: photo.name, mediaStream: mediaStream);
+    } catch (e) {
+      print(
+          "Error uploading file, trying again and requesting new permissions " +
+              e.toString());
+      await signOutGoogle();
+      await signInGoogle(
+          drivePermissions: true, drivePermissionsAttachments: true);
+      return await uploadFileToDrive(
+          fileBytes: fileBytes, fileName: photo.name, mediaStream: mediaStream);
+    }
+  }, onError: (e) {
+    openSnackbar(
+      SnackbarMessage(
+        title: "error-attaching-file".tr(),
+        description: e.toString(),
+        icon: appStateSettings["outlinedIcons"]
+            ? Icons.error_outlined
+            : Icons.error_rounded,
+      ),
+    );
+  });
+  if (result is String) return result;
+  return null;
+}
+
+Future<String?> getFileAndUpload() async {
+  dynamic result = await openLoadingPopupTryCatch(() async {
+    FilePickerResult? result = await FilePicker.platform.pickFiles();
+    if (result == null) throw ("no-file-selected".tr());
+
+    Uint8List fileBytes;
+
+    if (kIsWeb) {
+      fileBytes = result.files.single.bytes!;
+    } else {
+      File file = File(result.files.single.path ?? "");
+      fileBytes = await file.readAsBytes();
+    }
+
+    late Stream<List<int>> mediaStream;
+    mediaStream = Stream.value(fileBytes);
+
+    try {
+      return await uploadFileToDrive(
+        fileBytes: fileBytes,
+        fileName: result.files.single.name,
+        mediaStream: mediaStream,
+      );
+    } catch (e) {
+      print(
+          "Error uploading file, trying again and requesting new permissions " +
+              e.toString());
+      await signOutGoogle();
+      await signInGoogle(
+          drivePermissions: true, drivePermissionsAttachments: true);
+      return await uploadFileToDrive(
+        fileBytes: fileBytes,
+        fileName: result.files.single.name,
+        mediaStream: mediaStream,
+      );
+    }
+  }, onError: (e) {
+    print("Error");
+    openSnackbar(
+      SnackbarMessage(
+        title: "error-attaching-file".tr(),
+        description: e.toString(),
+        icon: appStateSettings["outlinedIcons"]
+            ? Icons.error_outlined
+            : Icons.error_rounded,
+      ),
+    );
+  });
+  if (result is String) return result;
+  return null;
+}
+
+Future<String?> uploadFileToDrive({
+  required Stream<List<int>> mediaStream,
+  required Uint8List fileBytes,
+  required String fileName,
+}) async {
+  if (googleUser == null) {
+    await signInGoogle(
+        drivePermissions: true, drivePermissionsAttachments: true);
+  }
+
+  final authHeaders = await googleUser!.authHeaders;
+  final authenticateClient = GoogleAuthClient(authHeaders);
+  final driveApi = drive.DriveApi(authenticateClient);
+
+  String folderName = "Cashew";
+  drive.FileList list = await driveApi.files.list(
+      q: "mimeType='application/vnd.google-apps.folder' and name='$folderName'");
+  String? folderId;
+  for (var file in list.files!) {
+    if (file.name == folderName) {
+      folderId = file.id;
+      break;
+    }
+  }
+
+  if (folderId == null) {
+    // If the folder doesn't exist, create it
+    drive.File folder = drive.File();
+    folder.name = folderName;
+    folder.mimeType = "application/vnd.google-apps.folder";
+    drive.File createdFolder = await driveApi.files.create(folder);
+    folderId = createdFolder.id;
+  }
+
+  if (folderId == null) throw ("Folder could not be created in Google Drive");
+
+  drive.Media media = new drive.Media(mediaStream, fileBytes.length);
+
+  drive.File driveFile = new drive.File();
+  final timestamp =
+      DateFormat("yyyy-MM-dd-hhmmss").format(DateTime.now().toUtc());
+  driveFile.name = timestamp + fileName;
+  driveFile.modifiedTime = DateTime.now().toUtc();
+  driveFile.parents = [folderId];
+
+  drive.File driveFileCreated =
+      await driveApi.files.create(driveFile, uploadMedia: media);
+
+  drive.Permission permission = drive.Permission();
+  permission.role = "reader";
+  permission.type = "anyone";
+  await driveApi.permissions.create(
+    permission,
+    driveFileCreated.id!,
+    sendNotificationEmail: false,
+  );
+
+  // Retrieve the updated metadata for the file with permissions
+  drive.File fileOnDrive = await driveApi.files.get(driveFileCreated.id!,
+      $fields: "id, name, webViewLink, permissions") as drive.File;
+
+  return fileOnDrive.webViewLink;
+}

diff --git a/budget/lib/widgets/util/onAppResume.dart b/budget/lib/widgets/util/onAppResume.dart
new file mode 100644
index 000000000..cedc88b7a
--- /dev/null
+++ b/budget/lib/widgets/util/onAppResume.dart
@@ -0,0 +1,53 @@
+import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
+
+class OnAppResume extends StatefulWidget {
+  const OnAppResume({
+    super.key,
+    required this.child,
+    required this.onAppResume,
+  });
+
+  final Widget child;
+  final VoidCallback onAppResume;
+
+  @override
+  State<OnAppResume> createState() => _OnAppResumeState();
+}
+
+class _OnAppResumeState extends State<OnAppResume> with WidgetsBindingObserver {
+  @override
+  void initState() {
+    super.initState();
+    WidgetsBinding.instance.addObserver(this);
+  }
+
+  @override
+  void dispose() {
+    WidgetsBinding.instance.removeObserver(this);
+    super.dispose();
+  }
+
+  AppLifecycleState? _lastState;
+  @override
+  void didChangeAppLifecycleState(AppLifecycleState state) {
+    super.didChangeAppLifecycleState(state);
+
+    if (_lastState == null) {
+      _lastState = state;
+    }
+
+    // app resumed
+    if (state == AppLifecycleState.resumed &&
+        (_lastState == AppLifecycleState.paused ||
+            _lastState == AppLifecycleState.inactive)) {
+      widget.onAppResume();
+    }
+
+    _lastState = state;
+  }
+
+  @override
+  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
+    return widget.child;
+  }
+}
